WE\u2019RE STILL INTERVIEWING WITNESSES AND THERE\u2019S NOT MUCH MORE TO REPORT OTHER THAN THAT IT WILL CONTINUE. &gt;&gt; Reporter: JAMES\u2019S FIRST ON CAMERA PUBLIC COMMENTS ON THE CASE ON A DAY WHEN THE GOVERNOR STAYED OUT OF SIGHT, PROMINENT DEMOCRATS CONTINUE TO CALL FOR HIS RESIGNATION. &gt;&gt; THE GOVERNOR HAS LOST THE CONFIDENCE OF HIS GOVERNING PARTNERS AND MANY NEW YORKERS, HE SHOULD STEP DOWN. &gt;&gt; Reporter: BUT CUOMO HAS SAID REPEATEDLY. &gt;&gt; I\u2019M NOT GOING TO REFINED. &gt;&gt; FORMER STAFFERS HAVE ACCUSED THE GOVERNOR OF SEXUAL HARASSMENT, ALLEGATIONS HE\u2019S DENIED, BUT TWO WEEKS AGO HE DID APOLOGIZE. &gt;&gt; I NOW UNDERSTAND THAT I ACTED IN A WAY THAT MADE PEOPLE FEEL UNCOMFORTABLE. &gt;&gt; Reporter: BUT CRITICS SAY THE GOVERNOR HAS LONG HAD A WAY OF USING WORDS THIS A HOSTILE MANNER. TODAY NEWS 4 OBTAINED NEW AUDIO OF A CONVERSATION BETWEEN CUOMO AND THE HEAD OF THE WORKING FAMILIES PARTY IN 2018 AFTER THE PROGRESSIVE GROUP INFORMED HIM THEY\u2019D RELUCTANTLY BACK HIM AS AN ALTERNATIVE TO THE REPUBLICAN NOMINEE. &gt;&gt; IF YOU EVER SAY, WELL, HE\u2019S BETTER THAN A REPUBLICAN AGAIN, I\u2019M GOING TO SAY YOU\u2019RE BETTER THAN A CHILD RAPIST. HOW ABOUT THAT. &gt;&gt; Reporter: TODAY A QUO MOW AIDE SAID HE WAS BEING HYPERBOLIC TO ILLUSTRATE THE OFFENSIVE NATURE OF THE WFP\u2019S OWN NAME CALLING. THE MAYOR SAYING IT\u2019S A TOXIC ATTITUDE GONE TOO FAR. &gt;&gt; THAT\u2019S WHAT I\u2019VE SEEN PLAYING OUT NOW, BUT IT\u2019S ALL BEHAVIOR WE\u2019VE SEEN DIFFERENT VERSIONS OF BEFORE THAT\u2019S JUST GOTTEN WORSE AND WORSE. &gt;&gt; Reporter: BUT CUOMO AIDE INSISTS THE GOVERNOR KOOPTING WITH INVESTIGATIONS AND FOCUSING ON HIS JOB, AN ASSERTION THAT GOT CONFIRMATION FOR ANDREA LEWIS COUSINS WHO TODAY SAID SHE IS COMMUNICATING WITH THE GOVERNOR. &gt;&gt; WE DID SPEAK ABOUT THE BUDGET, YES. I THINK PEOPLE IN NEW YORK EXPECT FOR US TO DO WHAT WE ARE SUPPOSED TO BE DOING AND THAT\u2019S WHERE WE\u2019RE FOCUSED. &gt;&gt; Reporter: NEWS 4 HAS REACHED OUT DIRECTLY TO THE GOVERNOR\u2019S OFFICE AND TO HIS LEGAL TEAM FOR A RESPONSE TO THE LATEST \&quot;NEW YORK TIMES\&quot; STORY ALLEGING THIS ALLEGED HARASSMENT BY A CURRENT EMPLOYEE. THREE THAT ARE BEING HELD IN PATTERSON. &gt;&gt;&gt; GETTING THE VACCINE TO UNDERSERVED COMMUNITIES HAS BEEN AN ISSUE SINCE THE SHOTS BECAME FIRST AVAILABLE. IN BERGEN COUNTY, SEVERAL ORGANIZATIONS HAVE COME TOGETHER TO HELP INOCULATE MEMBERS OF THE RAMAPOUGH LENAPE NATION. HOW THE NATIVE AMERICAN TRIBE IS PUTTING ASIDE CENTURIES OF DISTRUST OF THE GOVERNMENT FOR THE GREATER GOOD. &gt;&gt; THEY\u2019RE THE INDIGENOUS PEOPLE OF THE RAMAPOUGH MOUNTAINS, THEIR HISTORY DISTORTED, OMITTED AND LARKGELY IGNORED. IT WAS THE TRIBE WHO CHANGED THE COURSE OF THE REVOLUTIONARY WAR. &gt;&gt; OUR ANCESTORS ALLOWED THE REBELS -- GEORGE WASHINGTON USED THE RAMAPOUGH PASS. IT LITERALLY ELIMINATED ANY FORM OF STRATEGIC ADVANTAGE OR SURPRISE IN DEFENDING THE NEW ENGLAND COLONIES. &gt;&gt; THAT HISTORY LESSON COMES INTO SHARP FOCUS WITH THE JAB OF A NEEDLE AS DOZENS OF DESCENDANTS OF THOSE NATIVE AMERICANS RECEIVED THEIR FIRST DOSE OF THE COVID VACCINE ON THEIR OWN LAND. BERGEN COUNTY BRINGING A MOBILE CLINIC TO THE TRIBAL COMMUNITY CENTER ATOP THE MOUNTAIN DELIVERING MUCH MORE THAN A SHOT IN THE ARM. &gt;&gt; IT\u2019S HISTORIC IN A LOT OF WAYS, YOU KNOW. THERE HAS ALWS BEEN A FEELING THAT THE RAMAPOUGH ARE NOT SEEN HERE, THAT THE MOUNTAIN PEOPLE ARE NOT SEEN HERE, AND NEGATIVE STEREOTYPES, AND ALL OF THESE PEOPLE COME TO SAY THEY\u2019RE GOING TO LEND THEIR SUPPORT. THIS IS A MOMENTOUS DAY FOR US. &gt;&gt; Reporter: NEW BRIDGE MEDICAL CENTER ADMINISTERED NEARLY 50 VACCINES IN THE FIRST OF THREE PLANNED VISITS HERE. BERGEN COUNTY\u2019S COVID EQUITY TEAM THE DRIVING FORCE TO REACH THESE UNDERSERVED COMMUNITIES. &gt;&gt; BECAUSE SO MUCH OF THE APPOINTMENT AND REGISTRATION PROCESS IS HAPPENING ONLINE, ANYBODY ON THE WRONG SIDE OF THE DIGITAL DIVIDE IS LEFT OUT, AND SO WE\u2019VE BEEN FIGHTING TO GET APPOINTMENTS AND TO MAKE SURE THAT THERE ARE APPOINTMENTS FOR PEOPLE WHO WILL STRUGGLE TO GET APPOINTMENTS FOR THEMSELVES. &gt;&gt; WE\u2019LL BE BACK FOR THREE WEEKS IN A ROW, AND I MADE A COMMITMENT TO THE CHIEF THAT WE CAN COME UP HERE TO PROVIDE MEDICAL SERVICES OR EDUCATIONAL SERVICES FOR THE PEOPLE HERE. &gt;&gt; Reporter: VALERIE GUN AT A YOUNG 69 HAS BEEN ELIGIBLE FOR WEEKS, BUT COMING HERE WAS IN HER COMFORT ZONE. &gt;&gt; I THINK A LOT OF THE PROBLEMS IS FEAR OR PEOPLE GIVE UP, AND SO WHAT WE TRY TO DO WAS WE JUST KEEP SENDING POSITIVE VIBES OUT TO EVERYBODY, TELL THEM YOU CAN\u2019T GIVE UP. YOU GOT TO KEEP TRYING NO MATTER WHAT. BUT I AM SO HAPPY THAT I GOT MY SHOT, AND I INTEND TO TELL EVERYBODY YOU HAVE TO GET THE SHOT. &gt;&gt; THE RAMAPOUGH LAENAPE MOUNTAI HAVE NATION HAVE LIVED IN THE MOUNTAINS FOR HUNDREDS OF YEARS. VISITS FROM GOVERNMENT AGENCIES NEY DO NOT BRING GOOD NEWS BUT THIS DAY THEY HOPE CAN SIGNAL A CHANGE. &gt;&gt; AS I SAID TO THE CHIEF, WE NEED TO DO BETTER IN MAKING SURE THAT YOU ARE INCLUDED, AND THAT\u2019S MY COMMITMENT, AND TODAY IS THE START OF THAT. &gt;&gt; IT\u2019S BEEN A REAL ROUGH SLOG, AND LIKE YOU SAID, THIS IS A REAL CELEBRATION. 		function CreateEvent(type, data) {
			var event;

			if ('undefined' === typeof data) {
				data = {};
			}

			try {
				event = new CustomEvent(type, { detail: data });
			} catch (err) {
				event = document.createEvent('CustomEvent');
				event.initCustomEvent(type, true, true, data);
			}

			return event;
		}
	})();
